The core interface is defined in GroupCoordinator.java, which specifies the contract for group coordination operations including JoinGroupRequest and SyncGroupRequest handling for both classic and modern (consumer, streams, share) group protocols, and heartbeat management.\\n\\n## Group State Machine\\nThe classic group protocol uses a finite state machine defined in ClassicGroupState.java with five states:\\n- Empty: Group has no members, awaiting new members\\n- PreparingRebalance: Members are joining, group is preparing for rebalance\\n- CompletingRebalance: Leader has provided assignment, awaiting sync from all members\\n- Stable: All members are synchronized with assignments\\n- Dead: Group is being deleted\\n\\nState transitions are validated in ClassicGroupState.java (lines 111-117) which define valid previous states for each state.\\n\\n## Request Handlers\\nThe request flow is orchestrated through:\\n1.
